	country_credit_rating_actualized = {
		scope = country
		saved_scopes = {
			player_country
		}

		is_shown = {
			always = yes
		}

		is_valid = {
			always = yes
		}

		effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
					has_modifier = has_financial_center
				}
				country_credit_rating = yes
				sovereign_bond_yields = yes
			}
			country_rating_A_list = yes
			country_rating_B_list = yes
			country_rating_C_list = yes
			country_rating_D_list = yes
		}
	}

	market_gui_market_currency_list = {
		saved_scopes = { list_order list_filter }
		effect = {
			clear_global_variable_list = gui_market_currency_list
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:list_filter
				}
				market = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = var:gui_filter
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								var:gui_filter = scope:list_filter }
								set_variable = {
									name = gui_filter
									value = 0
								}
							}
						else = {
							set_variable = {
								name = gui_filter
								value = scope:list_filter
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						set_variable = {
							name = gui_filter
							value = scope:list_filter
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:list_order
				}
				market = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = var:gui_order
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								var:gui_order = scope:list_order
							}
							set_variable = {
								name = gui_order value = {
									subtract = scope:list_order
								}
							}
						}
						else = {
							set_variable = {
								name = gui_order
								value = scope:list_order
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						set_variable = {
							name = gui_order
							value = scope:list_order
						}
					}
				}
			}

			ordered_market_goods = {
				limit = {
					market_goods_is_currency = yes
					# OR = {
					# 	AND = {  }
					# 	AND = {  market_goods_is_industrial = yes }
					# }
				}

				min = 0
				add_to_global_variable_list = { name = gui_market_currency_list target = THIS }
			}
		}
	}

	market_gui_market_financial_product_list = {
		saved_scopes = { list_order list_filter }
		effect = {
			clear_global_variable_list = gui_market_financial_product_list
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:list_filter
				}
				market = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = var:gui_filter
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								var:gui_filter = scope:list_filter }
								set_variable = {
									name = gui_filter
									value = 0
								}
							}
						else = {
							set_variable = {
								name = gui_filter
								value = scope:list_filter
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						set_variable = {
							name = gui_filter
							value = scope:list_filter
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:list_order
				}
				market = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = var:gui_order
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								var:gui_order = scope:list_order
							}
							set_variable = {
								name = gui_order value = {
									subtract = scope:list_order
								}
							}
						}
						else = {
							set_variable = {
								name = gui_order
								value = scope:list_order
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						set_variable = {
							name = gui_order
							value = scope:list_order
						}
					}
				}
			}

			ordered_market_goods = {
				limit = {
					market_goods_is_financial_product = yes
				}

				min = 0
				add_to_global_variable_list = { name = gui_market_financial_product_list target = THIS }
			}
		}
	}

	trade_balance_actualized = {
		scope = country

		is_shown = {
			always = yes
		}

		is_valid = {
			always = yes
		}

		effect = {
			root = {
				set_variable = {  #stock
					name = trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
					value = trade_balance_in_gold
				}
				set_variable = { #flux
					name = trade_balance_in_gold_delta_fix
					value = trade_balance_in_gold_delta
				}
				set_variable = { #flux
					name = export_value_in_gold_week_fix
					value = export_value_in_gold_week
				}
				set_variable = { #flux
					name = import_value_in_gold_week_fix
					value = import_value_in_gold_week
				}
				trade_balance_0 = yes

				#####################################################################################################################
				#####################################################################################################################
				#####################################################################################################################
				#####################################################################################################################
				#####################################################################################################################
				#####################################################################################################################
				#####################################################################################################################

				#dinar
				if = {
					limit = {
						money_value_dinar > 0
						export_to_dinar > 0
					}
					set_variable = {
						name = export_in_dinar_in_gold_fix
						value = {
							add = export_in_dinar
							multiply = money_value_dinar_related_to_country_law #money_value_dinar
						}
					}
				}
				#dinar_algerian_dinar
				if = {
					limit = {
						money_value_dinar_algerian_dinar > 0
						export_to_dinar_algerian_dinar > 0
					}
					set_variable = {
						name = export_in_dinar_algerian_dinar_in_gold_fix
						value = {
							add = export_in_dinar_algerian_dinar
							multiply = money_value_dinar_algerian_dinar_related_to_country_law #money_value_dinar_algerian_dinar
						}
					}
				}
				#dinar_iraqi_dinar
				if = {
					limit = {
						money_value_dinar_iraqi_dinar > 0
						export_to_dinar_iraqi_dinar > 0

						name = export_in_dinar_iraqi_dinar_in_gold_fix

					}
				}

							add = export_in_dinar_libyan_dinar

					}
				}
				#dinar_moroccan_dirham
				if = {
					limit = {
						money_value_dinar_moroccan_dirham > 0
						export_to_dinar_moroccan_dirham > 0

	central_bank_debt_buyer_list_clear = {
		scope = country

		effect = {
			central_bank_debt_buyer_list_clear = yes
			central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_clear = yes 
		}
	} 


	actualise_trade_balance_value_for_comparaison = {
		scope = country
		saved_scopes = {
			player_country
		}

		is_shown = {
			always = yes
		}

		is_valid = {
			always = yes
		}

		effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
					market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
					export_value_in_currency > 0
					import_value_in_currency > 0 
				}

				set_variable = { #flux
					name = trade_balance_convert_gold_fix
					value = trade_balance_convert_gold
				}
				set_variable = {  #stock
					name = debt_in_national_currency_convert_gold_fix
					value = debt_in_national_currency_convert_gold
				}
				set_variable = { #flux
					name = excess_foreign_state_currency_convert_gold_fix
					value = excess_foreign_state_currency_convert_gold
				} 

			} 
		}
	}
#brace

################################################################################################################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

################################################################################################################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

#brace
	currency_exchange_panel_visibility = {
		is_shown = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root = yes
			not = {
				has_modifier = foreign_exchange_controls
			}
		}
	}
	no_currency_exchange_panel_visibility = {
		is_shown = {
			or = {
				has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = no
				market_owner_is_root = no
				has_modifier = foreign_exchange_controls
			}
		}
	}

	law_debt_currency_exchange_regime_visibility = {
		is_valid = {
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
			has_technology_researched = debt_currency_exchange_regime
			# not = {
			# 	is_subject = yes
			# }
			#has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}
		is_shown = {
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
			has_technology_researched = debt_currency_exchange_regime
			# not = {
			# 	is_subject = yes
			# }
			#has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}
	}

	gold_balance = {
		is_shown = {
			has_central_bank_FS_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root = yes
		}
	}
	no_gold_balance = {
		is_shown = {
			or = {
				has_central_bank_FS_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = no
				market_owner_is_root = no
			}
		}
	}

	national_debt = {
		is_shown = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root = yes
		}
	}
	no_national_debt = {

# variable_list_sorter

################################################################################################################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

#brace
	cv_sort_by_country_gdp = {
	scope = country
	saved_scopes = {
	player_country
	}

	is_shown = {
	always = yes
	}

	is_valid = {
	always = yes
	}

	effect = {
	scope:player_country = {
		clear_variable_list = list_before_order
		every_in_list = {
			variable = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
			scope:player_country = {
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = list_before_order
					target = prev
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
		if = {
			limit = {NOT = { has_variable = fi_sort_by_country_rank } }
			ordered_in_list = {
				variable = list_before_order
				order_by = owner.gdp
				max = 1000
				check_range_bounds = no
				scope:player_country = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = fi_sort_by_country_rank
		}
		else = {
			ordered_in_list = {
				variable = list_before_order
				order_by = { value = 0 subtract = owner.gdp}
				max = 1000
				check_range_bounds = no
				scope:player_country = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			remove_variable = fi_sort_by_country_rank
		}
		clear_variable_list = list_before_order
	}
	}
	}

	cv_sort_by_currency_value = {

					limit = {NOT = { has_variable = fi_sort_by_country_rank } }
					ordered_in_list = {
						variable = list_before_order
						order_by = owner.gdp
						max = 1000
						check_range_bounds = no
						scope:player_country = {
							add_to_variable_list = {
								name = dependent_economies_list_ordered_1
								target = prev
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = fi_sort_by_country_rank
				}
				else = {
					ordered_in_list = {
						variable = list_before_order
						order_by = { value = 0 subtract = owner.gdp}
						max = 1000
						check_range_bounds = no
						scope:player_country = {
							add_to_variable_list = {
								name = dependent_economies_list_ordered_1
								target = prev
							}
						}
					}
					remove_variable = fi_sort_by_country_rank
				}
				clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			}
		}
	}

							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				clear_variable_list = exports_imports_variable_list_1
				if = {
					limit = {NOT = { has_variable = fi_sort_by_country_rank } }
					ordered_in_list = {
						variable = list_before_order
						order_by = delta_value
						max = 1000
						check_range_bounds = no
						scope:player_country = {
							add_to_variable_list = {
								name = exports_imports_variable_list_1
								target = prev
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = fi_sort_by_country_rank
				}
				else = {
					ordered_in_list = {
						variable = list_before_order
						order_by = { value = 0 subtract = delta_value}
						max = 1000
						check_range_bounds = no
						scope:player_country = {
							add_to_variable_list = {
								name = exports_imports_variable_list_1
								target = prev
							}
						}
					}
					remove_variable = fi_sort_by_country_rank
				}
				clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			}
		}
	}
